et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press on my hand, but make it wide as in an odorant.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And said an old man that no one uses the fire cauterization similar to the razor, and the soldering iron and put them between the ribs, until it comes to the abscess;
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And so the fire burns the pain, as we have said in the passage about the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is great fear for the sick, or they are dead now, or a fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of mice.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you cure the mouse disease, of which we have said in the divisions of the treatments, and it does not benefit, then they assert that there are three ways of cautery that all are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	From which one has a certain method that you make three cauteries, or four, binding according to the length of the mouse, according to the figure of the fire liver treatment as we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand too hard on the cautery, and let the patients lie on their back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another method of cautery is that you heat the cautery to two points, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and let the wound be tied in place, or if the wound is on the side nearest to the left, and tie the elevations accordingly, according to the wound, according to the length of the body, and the cautery as much as the breadth of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Instruct the patient to put 2 fingers in the burn until the pain is perceived on the other side, and then apply fire to the cautery, and so four times.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see, that it burns all the cautery to three fingers.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has been soiled with rot for a long time, and this is what we said before.
de ydropisie	Fever of dropsies.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Fire is not good for dropsy, except when applied to the way called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure according to the ways we have said in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is fitting that you make four cauterizations inside the wound, on the stomach, on the liver, on the liver again, two behind the back under the spine, and one under the knee;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and so the cauterizations are well near the spot of the wound.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leave the cauterization to open for a long time due to putrid flesh, and do not give up on the patient's cure after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would hasten, and both kinds of intentions would come together with God's aid.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the abdomen is like the claw that we have previously shown.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And this one on the back should be olive-like, as it was placed there before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical and contain a lot of pus like citron, it is necessary to cauterize on the back between the little finger and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery, as if to turn.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, otherwise it will melt like fire, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After do this for both legs, two cauterizations on each leg at the point of the little knife.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the fire cautery be applied to the long ones, one in front of the knee joint and the other behind it, in the thigh.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and let them remain long enough to heal what's inside.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the treatment of other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	of the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When stomach and intestines are inflamed due to cold and moisture, where the virtues of digestion and retention that are found in the stomach and intestine are deficient, and cannot be cured with other remedies.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering much and with strong flatulence, so do you apply fire cautery on the stomach as he spoke of it before, or to the cauterization of the stomach, in order.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and 4 cauteries are done under the subtle nose to all cautery needles, and 2 cauteries above the joints.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see the moistors abundant and the patient suffering, perform fire cautery on the fingernail, and fire cautery on each joint, and two times fire cautery on the stomach beneath the great one, because the cure is beneficial when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids.
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are on the fundament or one or more and are ancient and of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, but it does not profit, then do cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the spine of the back, those who are entirely behind the lower vertebrae and are a little bit in front in a triangular shape, and one cautery under the nose twice.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think his stomach is chilled and the meat does not cook, and the face swells up, then one cautery on the stomach, as it has been said, and one more above the liver, and one more above the spleen to all needle cauteries.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the fire cautery be held for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment let the limb be healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness which is called "theelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you bind the limb, if it seems like a razor has been applied to it, and then set it on fire completely over the limb that was bound.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand be left so the cautery comes to the base of the vein, because it is sterile.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once more, and if there is much swelling of the limb, cautery each part as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the application of ointments, until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you set a great cautery on the swollen place, it will have even greater relief.
de plaie mal curee	of badly treated wounds
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patients cannot endure a lance or an opening, what we will tell him in his own tongue, if it comes to this illness that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is a fistula and it has become inflamed, decayed, and putrid due to moisture and corruption, if you examine it thoroughly, and notice how deep it goes.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After the cauterization which seems like a razor, and pours it into the fistula according to the quantity that has entered, and repeats the cautery until the body is scorched and corrupted once, or twice, or three times, as much as the amount of blood needed;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of tearing the nerve that is inflamed, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the body of the intestine and into the colon, be cautious with these things, and do not make fire that only burns in a walnut, and suppose they are not human.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after curing the animal until it is completely healed, and if the lesions are cleaned and the matter has long been discharged, then you know that the animal has completely recovered.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the material is not bone, then know that it is hard, and corrupted the bone at its form;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as of one such thing which we will speak about in his place.
de la maladie des reins	of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from frost comes to the joints, and great swelling, and does not take hold of a woman, then it is fitting that you apply fire cautery on both sides of the joint from which frost has come, using the clavicle cautery that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if the cauterized area is in the middle, then three cauteries are to be done in line, and this will bring greater relief.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and swollen from frost and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make fire cautery in the part behind the bladder, where the hair of the groin meets, and left and right, each one to be cauterized as long as possible like.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And let the fire cautery be done for his back, or if he has need of it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let them cut the clavicle in the shape as previously said.
de la marris	of the gallbladder
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the flesh is cold and moist, and will not conceive, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends late.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, it feels great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore it is fitting that one should make three fire cauteries around the wound, as we have said in the fire cautery of the bladder, and let them cut the flesh behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and also they should cut the clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	From the hunch
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the moist viscous discharge descends to the joint of the hunchback, and because of this it remains still, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	And it is found that the joints are swollen in the departure of flesh, so it is fitting that you cauterize the patient on the skin of the flank with fire cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the joint as it turns, so that the skin is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cautery is like those applied to the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, then let the three cauteries be made of olive oil, and do them as well as all the wounds.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal him so that he is cured.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain of the groin
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the skin of the flank, and it's from cold and moisture, and the patients are cured by what we said in the division, and the treatment does not work, and the illness is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary to cleanse the patient of the thick humors of rotten pills or other hard-sounding pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After applying the fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of cautery is according to two kinds:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	which means applying medicine in an assembly and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many ways, of which one is such that:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the root of the hawthorn, or apply three cauteries in a triangular form, and make them deep and broad, with space between each cautery equal to twice the thickness of an ox's hide, and let there be olive oil cauteries.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never is cautery performed at noon above the nape of the neck, for there are four times according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, so that the cauterizing at the cauterization of the circle which we have before said in the dislocation of the shoulder.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but cut in such a way that the circles contain all the shoulder, and all the thickness of the bone be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way to do it in sciatik, when the pain stays in the haunch and does not reach as far as the thigh or as far as the knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes just above the thigh and the knee, so that they do two cauterizations in the place where the patient says the pain is, and four cauterizations above the ankle on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and if they are cauterized with a knife, and burn the thickness of the bone.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain spreads just to two or four feet away from where they cut, they should cauterize it where they feel the pain three times or four times, which is called "pain".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if that happens, if they make more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the patient feels that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, they should cauterize using the cutlery or circular cautery, and be very careful in all your cauteries not to let the cautery burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause the patient more great nuisance and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen others who had fire applied to the ankle on the foot, and they let it burn so that the leg was entirely bare, and also the foot, and it became perceived and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a treatment of the abdomen that led to death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	If the pains are in both upper and lower parts together, do fire cauterization in one and the other.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones said in the cautery of hawthorn, thus is the manner, make a tool like that one and put it at the head as big as a nail of thumb, or just a little less, and place it between cuts, alternating from one cut to another, with space equal to the size of a single thread.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let them intertwine in two parts, and let them also be like our own, and have one iron band made well.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is completely red and filled with splinters, and then put it on the side of the sick man's joint, and turn towards his healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let him wait three days after the cautery is done.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply plaster of butter, and let the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with ointment until he is cured.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Al-Bucayr ibn Fayrum says that we should use this cautery sparingly because of the danger of its effects, and few people dare to do so.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	And all these are good cauterizations, which he can endure, and at that moment when he is most affected.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of medicine burns so that you make an instrument between crossways, in which the blade descends along the edge of the wound, and is either iron or flint with a long appearance, and has two on each side, and has the quantity equal to the thickness of two bucks.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and be over twice as long and twice as wide, and they join together in the same form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the hedge of hawthorn on the patient lying on his chest side, and pressing your hand much above the hedge of thorns;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing between the two circles of hot water which is heated over one pot, and letting him suffer for an hour or thereabouts, and endure the heat and the fever.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For the fire cautery, he finds a morsuration just like from the fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the morsurations have not healed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the heel on a gentle poultice, and let it remain for three days, and apply butter until the black scab is shed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him remain for three days to be purified by the strait.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and that would be the rear support after the treatment of ointments until he is cured.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended up to the thigh or up to the knee, he will do the same instrument which you used more frequently;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the method of the cauterizing fire, and I have written it in order to treat on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take calomel and quicksilver, equal amounts of both, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where if there is a small opening that does not prevent the point of an arrow from entering.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put the two pots in another pot that is very heavy, and put on calicum and chalk and hot water above, until it has two above the powders, then you will have well pierced with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until the hot water and ashes come down from above the heavy pot, then take all that hot water, and pour it onto chalk and calicum as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And when it is very hot and has been made with the work of medicine and cauterization on other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For all operations with fire, and if they also use other medicines such as the fiery substance, if it is applied to the root of the hair like cauterization, and honey, acacia tree juice, and alum with soap, all these things combined together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galiens tells us of a cure from which one man was cured of the pain in his groin and sciatic nerve, and great praise, and says that no other cure is needed, and he became well only once when this cure was performed, and he would bathe as he instructs here afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And thus in some manner you press with the lardigre a green and fresh vert, and pound it out with a little of fat, and put on the root and on the thigh or where the pain lies, and bind.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and let him stay for three hours and by the quantity that the patient feels no burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then put it in a bath so that the body becomes a little red, and put him in the litter, and the pain will depart all and he will be well.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And instructs that no one should use cauterization of such medicine after evacuation.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with sheep's intestines, if it helps.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and must be done the cautery in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take a linen cloth and anoint it with old oil, and place it on the fossa between the big toe and the little toe called the scrotum.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dried mutton fat, and applying it to the wound with fire until it becomes charcoal, put linen over it and leave it there until it is stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and repeat this in the same way, and do not cease to do so until you think that it has come close enough to the heel, and the pain is gone.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this method of cauterization is called "cautery with mutton fat".
de la dolor dou dos	of the painful back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or by percussion or by too great evacuation, or by the appearance of something spread out cold matter, none of these similarities is worth cautery, except for that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is therefore after this that the patient must void foul matter or other similar things, and upon his back, if the pain lies, three lines marked of encaustic, and in each line a cautery or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let it be made the cautery according to the cautery which is called "poins
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three cauteries or four at the cauterium with a straight-clawed knife according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This sickness often comes in young children, and the signs of its beginning are when they have a narrow shoulder when they move, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the lower spine at the back of the neck, and on it, the appearance that appears on other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and want to treat it, if you cauterize with the cautery of the cell according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cautery is purple on each part of the spine, increasing.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if you cauterize inside the spine at the puncture point one or two lines deep and so that the points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the treatment, keep the patient so that they are healthy as we have said, and guard so that you do not introduce cautery into a swollen gland which is in the grip of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	From the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain from joints occurs due to moist spots that are expanded in each limb of the body, and when pain comes to the foot, they call it "podagre" properly, and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cautery in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the patient cut off all hair around the joint of the foot, and let it be olive oil according to this shape:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a spot that you prick on the face of the foot, make a cautery all around the point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to each knee and other joints, and this happens often, let him cut cauterization on each knee 3 cauterizations or 4 from each part, with all olive oil:
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you have a need for more, then do more, but not hold your hand over the fire longer than until the thick part of the cure is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend just to the genitals and the back, administer the fire cautery that we have said in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if pains are in the hands, then cut points into the wrist 2 lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains no pain in the fingers, then cut points on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come to these spots or joints so that they will heal, cauterize each part, and do good governance for the patient and give them medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good governance and purge the phlegm, he will be made healthy by God's aid.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the surgical cut of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the groin and the bowels descend into the grooves it is new, so it's fitting that when treating wounded eyes, you should not apply ointment the same day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and if they use things that make the belly empty, so that the fetuses descend from the womb;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after that seat the patient on his back between your hands, and he commands that you tie off his leg so that the bleeding stops, and bring it to your hands, and sew over the rupture on the bone of the finger, and do a sign such as a half circle above the bone.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	The fire cautery comes from this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and has stopped bleeding.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then remove the bowels at their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and keep the ministrants from holding back when they return.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and operate well on the patient, and put on him a garter and a servant over the knees, and another over the leg that holds back his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then apply the cautery to the marked place on all hands, and hold right and left until you strike bone, and if you do not hit it the first time, then it will recur again another time until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and beware subtly that the boiling blood does not escape while you are doing the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	you must not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient may not die from this illness or another.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	and it is fitting that the cautery for children should be subtle according to their measure, and for big people also big according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days of treatment, remove the burned part with lard until it falls off;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the treatment of other ointments until they are healed, and rest the sick on their back for 40 days so that the wound is well closed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is fitting that his necessities be provided for a long time, so that the boils do not burst when he goes out to chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, he must be presented with a well-made bandage, and then for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and good rest, that he may work little and be warned of too much drinking and eating, and of eating too high;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and if he follows this teaching, then he becomes entirely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after your cutting treatment of the cautery.
de la routure dou ventre	of the cut on the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When swellings come in other places and are recognized, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and burn off one-third of the wound.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients ever said that one must apply the fire cautery to three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the level of the incision and make a line for the width above the cut, and another below it; and with your finger press around the entire edge of the cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and less severe.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, or from a fall or from injuring it, and the pain lasts for a long time, and medicine cures are useless, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cautery that is called "poins," and do the cauterizations according to the length of the limb, its thickness, and its weakness, and its virtue, and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If he is whole after the first cautery, this is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	So that the name of this procedure is repeated because it is necessary to do another cautery on that same part, since it must be done on the member that is nearest to it, for that reason you should perform the cauteries until the patient is whole.
de meselerie	of incompetence
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The problem is treated with no success by cautery for great help, and the same malady that comes from the putrefaction of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can you see the cautery applied, take care if the patient is at the beginning of a disease, and apply it according to what we have said in division, and do not remove or stay in place, for that reason be cautious that the corruption does not spread throughout the whole patient, then perform cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	Apply a new cautery to the head and the other side near the forehead.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and 2 above the 2 horns, and 1 behind on the heel.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and hold your hand so that the cautery comes alive just to the bone, and so that the scabs come out in great numbers, so that the vapors of the large humors can issue forth.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if there are many swellings everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and they are manifestly inflamed, so it is fitting that you use the cauterizing cauteries we have discussed, and 5 cauterize in the nose, and 2 on the spine of the neck, and 6 on the spine of the back, and 1 on the cramp and 1 other part, and 2 on each shoulder;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and there is swelling on the thighs, and swelling on the tendons of the foot, and on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the cavities of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of nails that are under the groin bone, lest they be burned.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never do cautery on the bone of the thumb, and also on the bone of the stomach, and also on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when you do more cautery, you also give more relief and profit.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the sick do not feel any pain from cautery as much as they would if they were healthy, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is fitting that cauterization should be large and small according to the members and joints, as you will find in various ways with the iron tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment let him be left of flour powder mixed with honey and other remedies until he is made whole.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it's not healed, then you should do fire cautery on the member according to its size and thinness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and if the fire cautery is only slightly entering into the swollen flesh.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes it is done by hand and with the foot and on the back, at the end of the nerve that muffles the member, and so if the swelling remains.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and beware that no one interferes in this if he is not acquainted with the limbs and the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	of scars.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness called "albaras" is old and weak, and the doctors' medicines are of no use, then apply cautery with a cautery one point at a time, according to the quantity of the wound's depth, until the bleeding stops and changes its color.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then feed the patient with flour and dates and lentils mixed with olive oil and leaves of plantain, and blood from the gallbladder and blood from the gizzard, each one a portion.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let all this be mixed together, and tie it up in a cloth, and pour it into the patient as long as he is well.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The doctor who pricks with fire
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the chancre comes at the beginning and you stop looking, prick it with fire that seems like a circle all around the turn of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all learned men agree that one should also apply cautery to the middle of a sore.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And so I do not think this is good, because I fear it will be ulcerous and corrupted, and I have wanted to avoid such things from the start;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And another thing is that the wounds should be cauterized internally, with a cautery called "circule", as we have mentioned in many other cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some have a disease called "adubelati", and it delays death or because of the swelling that it makes, or because the old man is thin when he is decrepit (that means he is very old), and has little blood, or because of age.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you should consider hastening his death;
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	so then cauterize him internally with many small cauterizations and pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards let him.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	She will soon die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you view her pierce with the fire cauterization, so that the cauterized form is like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the midst of this disease which is called "adubelati" so that the cauterization has pierced the liver, and it should be such that the patient feels pain on both sides in this manner so that the course of the putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, so that he may be completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the burn cauterization by iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease that is called "corrodens", and it is no other than an injury to a limb, because it causes the limbs to rot as well as dry bones.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in one who can suffer fire cautery, then take the cauterization needles very small and large, according to what is needed for the patient or the illness.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	after cauterizing from all parts until you have reached the entire corruption, and nothing remains, then everything that is corrupted must be cut out.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let him lie for three days, and put on his cauterized wounds to suffer from a firebreak with oil until the escharatures of the fire are cut out, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the cure of bone-grown ulcers.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that no sick chariot is born, it is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if this does not happen, then resume the cauterization on that which has remained corrupted since.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method of treatment is never cured by medicine applied to the patient, through fire cauterization.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But all the fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already said the cure for the ailing one in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take the amount you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of worms that come to the bone
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that on the bone by chance there is born a disease which we call "clos" according to our intention, and it is a great thing to blame that causes the pain.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And there are two kinds of fire cauteries for this disease.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery if you are going to cut the hair, just as one cuts the nail, and make it of good iron, to the measure that can pierce the thorn through all parts, and have subtle margins;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After put it on the head like a thorn, and turn your hand all around the thorn until it comes out from the head of the thorn;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it remain so for three days, till it starts to rot with pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of fresh mallows crushed with thread, and put the poultice on the entire area overnight, and the thorn will come out and be dislodged from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let his hair grow long and even.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by force of the body, and it happens many times in hands and feet, then you must apply fire cautery to hot water.
et est en teil maniere:	and is done in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a thorn from a rose or iron, or a quill of vinegar, and set it on the warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and set the thorn so that it bleeds all over, then put a little hot water in, and hold your hand tight, and press your hand turning so that the margin of the thorn comes to the root of the nail, so that the hot water can go deep down to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer for a little while under the heat of the water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then let him go as is, and he will rot to death all at his roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	In this manner do it after another, until you have searched through all those which are in the body, then treat the limbs that bind with strong bands.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment for the quiver
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some shiver with cold or fever of a quarter or any other, it is fitting that you make four cauteries on the spine at the back, one cautery between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cautery near it and one above the stomach at the olive cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	so that he will stop shivering and hasten his recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of dry sores or ulcers
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time do they appear without the body's internal baths, or dry sores/ulcers, that come from great corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if it is fitting that when they appear, you make a cautery over each head of the pustule;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery of fusel wood of myrtle, so that the point may be gripped by fire, or with a root of artemisia, long, or at the lenticular cautery;
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And at some point the cauterized ones are found to be broken when they first appear, following this manner; and they cannot grow again forward but are destroyed by the excess that comes from them, and heal.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary to do this after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when an artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often it happens that great bleeding of the artery occurs when the vein is cut at the wound, or at the incision of the abscess, or after cauterizing a member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very grievous to stink.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And for those who have it, when they come to know, if you hasten to put your two fingers on the wound of the vein, and pull it very tightly so that the swelling is not calmed down below your fingers, and no more pain comes from it;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then put in the fire the olive oil cauteries of various sizes until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then apply, be it a large or small one, according to the wound and where the artery is cut, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your thumb, and keep it there until the vein does not remain open.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the fire has disappeared when you lift your thumb off the vein, and the cautery has cooled down, then take it hastily another cautery which is on fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease doing this one after another until the vein is constricted.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is near, and that no other evil comes upon the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when the vein does not burst from the artery, it cannot be well constricted itself when the artery is large; unless this happens by one of the four ways we have previously mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	When or by cautery, when it is not treated, or by strong binding with thread, or by medicines applied which have power to constrict blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and bound and strained as a result.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will put a stop to the swelling of the tightly bound limb or putting things on it, or other similar things, if they do not profit from this.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to no one and he has not been treated with any medicine beforehand, then it must be put on a needle over the wound of the vein as we have said, and constricting so that blood is stopped from above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and he must not move, but his blood should be let off frequently, so that it becomes very cold, until the flesh is frozen and swollen and constricted.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and do this in front of those who have need of cautery and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book on treatments of cuts.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter of all diseases for which it is necessary to cauterize with fire or with hot medicine, the omissions and the causes and the strata and the forms of the cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed the second chapter on the nose with just one piece, and I will go to this same place in order to treat it more easily because we find it more conveniently.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so that I begin this, it is necessary, dear boy, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than with the first cautery, and therefore it must be done with greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter there are many times evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and because of this many fall into death.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to enter into folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	Because many ways of men come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If they come from such a place where they have been afflicted with their disease so that they quickly die from the force of what they find in themselves, and from the great size of their sickness;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from this must come fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of those who bring you the truth, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am cured.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the sick person is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting to trust only in those who come to you and have this manner, but put more consideration into your honor than your profit, and be neither too weak nor too foolish about what you are sure of and what you can obtain.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use divine prediction and signs in your treatments to see if the health is converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you achieve a good reputation, fame, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three dear sons, Our Lord gives you good understanding and truth, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I instruct you on this chapter in devising by chapters, according to what is before or in front of the cautery chapter, which I have devised for you from the head joint to the joints, because you will find it easier to deal with that which you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Fill the full head with water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is known that this illness often comes from children at birth, and when the child holds their head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it is caused by a return that we do not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness in fire except in children, and in all those that I have seen it has led to death.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason, I think that it is worth wasting the work in some treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child because the joint was swollen with water, and the head became heavy each day until it could no longer bear.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and he believed so strongly that he was dead, and this moisture had assembled beneath the bone on top of his spleen, between the liver and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the wounds are so severe if the moisture is between the liver and the bone, and the abscesses are small, that you must cut a large incision in his head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and so long as it is two times as deep as us, until the moisture runs out;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and you will see the form of a splinter:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the swelling is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, cut two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is below the bone, and you see the signs that occur in each part of the head, such as swelling of the commissures (the corners) of the mouth on both sides, and the pain increases when you press with your hand inside it, and this does not return:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you must break open his skull with three incisions according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After binding the incisions with cloth and powder, and then applying vinegar and oil, and leaving so for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then remove the dressing, and treat the wound with poultices and ointments, and let the head swell apart, then give the patient dry meat mixed with a little moisture until the limb is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incision is that you look at or open the swelling of the abscess and the assembly of the fluid;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because it does not happen often.
aucune fois derrier;	never again.
aucune fois en destre;	Sometimes in distress;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	The wound should be cut near or at the abscess opening, and the filling of the liquid, and the part according to what you have the power.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not cover the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and take away some blood, if so that the patient dies from the deterioration of the blood and moisture evacuation.
de reume	of flesh
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it happens that there is no disease which is called 'catarrh' in the eyes or on the skin, and the disease is old and medicine does not help, then the following remedy should be used: cut with cauterization as when you cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you cover your eyes, that the patient turns his head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the head with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then pull out the patient's neck from all of that cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	The patient will examine which vein is broken, and the veins of one and both are drawn behind the ears, and it does not heal soon.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then he will mark the veins of the elbow, and then cut one and both with a good spatula of two parts, until the vein reaches the bone, and that be in proportion to the size of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	If you see this, pour out the spatula under the artery and strike on top, in cutting as is necessary to traverse.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, it should be closed with a continuous downward flow of fire.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the arteries do not open to feel, so it is fitting that you measure the quantity of the space three doubs, then mark and cut until the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and that which is fitting to put fire in the wound if it is six cubits, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can suffer, and the replenishment of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on the bone at that spot, if it doesn't give pain to the surrounding flesh, then pull out what's causing the swelling and tie the wound shut, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	The body leaves
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the ancient body comes in and catarrh is present, due to moisture of tears and colds in the temples and old sores that resemble similar things, and he is treated with various medicines and remedies and none of these help him, we must extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize the ulcers, as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of extracting them is that the patient makes his hair stand up behind their temples, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its pulsing, and is not fully returned until many people who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is returned, then the patient tightens their neck with some strips, then rubs them with any harsh cloth, and raises the limb in warm water until the artery appears distinctly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Take the spatula of which this is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then scorch the leather lightly until you reach the artery, then tear it upwards by pinches, and pull well away from each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is subtle, then turn at the tip of the needle, then cut from that part according to the quantity of the two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not cut, do not separate it without pain throughout everything.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And pull out six cubits of flesh, just up to three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, it is advisable to tie in two fingers of a strong doubled thread of silk, lest purulence appears before the wound is sounded, and pus commences.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut the superfluity that is between the two joints in this hour itself, and then, if you see, if he cuts with the fire cautery of the sword just to the bone until the joint is cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and this is the mother work, if the patient does not have fever and he has a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the fire cautery is aid to finish off the moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater aid against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries, that one fills him with new cotton and puts a well-made tunic.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are cut open, you must cure him with dry medicines that make charcoal, and with tourniquets, until he is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	If without cut of the artery so that it does not bleed like you do when you work, then hurry to cover with cautery, or apply quick lead and strain it on your hand until it is not stained.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have that at hand, put it on the lead until it freezes, and bring the lead to cold water repeatedly, so strain it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and what is more thin and lighter in the extraction of an artery, then you should cauterize a vein with this cautery piercing to two parts, but pierce them well thick to hold its heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When the instruments are too dark, he holds less heat.
